title: "Properties (REPORT Object Model)"

# Properties

2198 properties from `ReportApi.chm`.

| Name | Summary |
| --- | --- |
| [`IRepArrowInt.ArrowHeadAtBegin`](ireparrowint-arrowheadatbegin.md) | Specifies which arrow tip DIAdem REPORT plots at the beginning of an arrow. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.ArrowHeadAtEnd`](ireparrowint-arrowheadatend.md) | Specifies which arrow tip DIAdem REPORT plots at the end of an arrow. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.Index`](ireparrowint-index.md) | Returns the index of an arrow in DIAdem REPORT. If you change the ZOrder property of an object, you also change the indexes of all objects. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.IsSelected`](ireparrowint-isselected.md) | Specifies whether an arrow is selected in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.Line`](ireparrowint-line.md) | Specifies how the line of an arrow is displayed in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.Name`](ireparrowint-name.md) | Specifies the name of a line or of an arrow in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.ObjectType`](ireparrowint-objecttype.md) | Specifies the object type in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.Position`](ireparrowint-position.md) | Specifies the position of an arrow in a DIAdem REPORT worksheet. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.TagStored`](ireparrowint-tagstored.md) | Specifies a tag for an object in DIAdem REPORT. Use this property to add additional information to the object. Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the object. The tag does not affect the behavior of the object. DIAdem saves this tag with the layout. |
| [`IRepArrowInt.TagTemporary`](ireparrowint-tagtemporary.md) | Specifies a temporary tag for an object in DIAdem REPORT. Use this property to add additional information to the object. Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the object. The tag does not affect the behavior of the object. DIAdem does not save this tag with the layout. |
| [`IRepArrowLineInt.Color`](ireparrowlineint-color.md) | Specifies the color of an arrow line in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepArrowLineInt.LineType`](ireparrowlineint-linetype.md) | Specifies the line type of an arrow line in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepArrowLineInt.Width`](ireparrowlineint-width.md) | Specifies the line width of an arrow line in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepArrowSubObjInt.Name`](ireparrowsubobjint-name.md) | Returns the name of the subobject of an arrow in DIAdem REPORT when DIAdem calls the event assigned to the OnArrow for ToolTipEvents property. DIAdem calls this event if you press the shift key and move the mouse over a REPORT object. |
| [`IRepArrowSubObjInt.Type`](ireparrowsubobjint-type.md) | Returns the subobject type of an arrow in DIAdem REPORT when DIAdem calls the event assigned to the OnArrow for ToolTipEvents property. DIAdem calls this event if you press the shift key and move the mouse over a REPORT object. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.Enable`](irepattributelistint-enable.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT uses the attribute list for the curve expansion in an axis system. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.LineStyles`](irepattributelistint-linestyles.md) | Specifies the properties of the lines of an expanding curve in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.UseLineColor`](irepattributelistint-uselinecolor.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays expanding curves in the colors specified in the attribute list. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.UseLineInterval`](irepattributelistint-uselineinterval.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays expanding curves in the intervals specified in the attribute list. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.UseLineType`](irepattributelistint-uselinetype.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays expanding curves with the line types specified in the attribute list. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.UseLineWidth`](irepattributelistint-uselinewidth.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays expanding curves in the line width specified in the attribute list. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.UseMarkerProperties`](irepattributelistint-usemarkerproperties.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays expanding curves with the marker properties specified in the attribute list. |
| [`IRepAttributeListInt.UseMarkerType`](irepattributelistint-usemarkertype.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays expanding curves with the markers specified in the attribute list. |
| [`IRepAxisLabelInt.Angle`](irepaxislabelint-angle.md) | Specifies the angle of the axis label in an axis system in DIAdem REPORT. DIAdem only includes the Angle property in the objects 3DAxisX , 3DAxisY , and 3DAxisZ if you assign the value FALSE to the UseLabelAutoAngle property. |
| [`IRepAxisLabelInt.Font`](irepaxislabelint-font.md) | Specifies the font of the axis label in an axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepAxisLabelInt.OffsetX`](irepaxislabelint-offsetx.md) | Specifies the margin of the axis label in the x-direction as a percentage of the width of the worksheet in DIAdem REPORT. First assign the value eAxisLabelRelativePositionManual to the property RelativePosition . |
| [`IRepAxisLabelInt.OffsetY`](irepaxislabelint-offsety.md) | Specifies the margin of the axis label in the y-direction as a percentage of the height of the worksheet in DIAdem REPORT. First assign the value eAxisLabelRelativePositionManual to the property RelativePosition . |
| [`IRepAxisLabelInt.RelativePosition`](irepaxislabelint-relativeposition.md) | Specifies the relative position of the axis label to the axis in an axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepAxisLabelInt.Text`](irepaxislabelint-text.md) | Specifies the axis label in an axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepAxisLabelInt.UseCurveColor`](irepaxislabelint-usecurvecolor.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT also assigns the curve color to the axis labels of the axis system. |
| [`IRepAxisLineInt.Color`](irepaxislineint-color.md) | Specifies the line color of an axis in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. DIAdem only includes the property Color if you assign the value FALSE to the UseCurveColor property. |
| [`IRepAxisLineInt.UseCurveColor`](irepaxislineint-usecurvecolor.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT also assigns the curve color to the axis of an axis system. You must assign the value TRUE to the property UseIndividualAxisStyle in order to use the UseCurveColor property. |
| [`IRepAxisLineInt.Width`](irepaxislineint-width.md) | Specifies the line width of an axis in an axis system in DIAdem REPORT. You must assign the value TRUE to the UseIndividualAxisStyle property in order to specify the line width of an axis. |
| [`IRepAxisMiniTickGridLineInt.Interval`](irepaxisminitickgridlineint-interval.md) | Specifies the interval and the length of the line sections of the broken minitick lines in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. Greater values mean greater intervals. |
| [`IRepAxisMiniTickGridLineInt.LineType`](irepaxisminitickgridlineint-linetype.md) | Specifies the line style of the miniticks in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepAxisMiniTickGridLineInt.Width`](irepaxisminitickgridlineint-width.md) | Specifies the line width of the minitick grid lines in an axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepAxisTickInt.Channel`](irepaxistickint-channel.md) | Specifies the tick channel of a 3D axis system or of a polar axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepAxisTickInt.Distance`](irepaxistickint-distance.md) | Specifies the interval between the ticks you want labeled in units of the axis range, in a 3D axis system or in polar axis system in DIAdem REPORT. If the scaling is not logarithmic, the value of the Distance property is the space between the main ticks you want to label. If the scaling is logarithmic, DIAdem interprets the values before the decimal point and the values after the decimal point of the Distance property separately. The integer value before the decimal point specifies the steps between two labels, which are powers of ten. For example, if the axis origin and the tick interval have the value 1, DIAdem labels the ticks at 10 0 , 10 1 , 10 2 and so on. For example, if you assign the value 3 to the tick interval, DIAdem labels the ticks at 10 0 , 10 3 , 10 6 and so on. The reciprocal value after the decimal point, specifies intervals that you want to label in the ranges defined by the value before the decimal point. For example, if you assign the value 1.25 to the Distance property, DIAdem divides the area into quarters. |
| [`IRepAxisTickInt.SpacingType`](irepaxistickint-spacingtype.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT takes the tick positions in an axis system from a data channel or calculates the tick positions automatically. |
| [`IRepBackgroundColorInt.ColorIndex`](irepbackgroundcolorint-colorindex.md) | Specifies the highlighting color of an object in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepBackgroundColorInt.GradientDirection`](irepbackgroundcolorint-gradientdirection.md) | Specifies the color shading direction of the highlighting color of an object in DIAdem REPORT. You also can use the SetFillingColor method to specify filling effects. Not all REPORT objects display filling effects. |
| [`IRepBackgroundColorInt.GradientMode`](irepbackgroundcolorint-gradientmode.md) | Specifies the color shading variant of the highlighting color of an object in DIAdem REPORT. You also can use the SetFillingColor method to specify filling effects. Not all REPORT objects display filling effects. |
| [`IRepBackgroundColorInt.RGB`](irepbackgroundcolorint-rgb.md) | Specifies the RGB values of a highlighting color in DIAdem REPORT. First assign the value eColorIndexOtherColors to the property ColorIndex . If you assign the value eColorIndexFillEffects to the property ColorIndex , the RGB property specifies the first color of a filling effect. You also can use the SetRGBColor method to specify individual colors. Use the SetFillingColor method to specify filling effects. Not all REPORT objects support filling effects. |
| [`IRepBackgroundColorInt.RGBFilling`](irepbackgroundcolorint-rgbfilling.md) | Specifies the RGB values of the second highlighting color of a color shading in DIAdem REPORT. First assign the value eColorIndexFillEffects to the property ColorIndex . The RGB property specifies the first color of a filling effect. You also can use the SetFillingColor method to specify filling effects. Not all REPORT objects support filling effects. |
| [`IRepBackgroundColorInt.Transparency`](irepbackgroundcolorint-transparency.md) | Specifies the transparency of a highlighting color as a percentage in DIAdem REPORT. The value 100 specifies a completely transparent display and the value 0 specifies a completely opaque display. Not all DIAdem objects display transparency. |

Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the object. The tag does not affect the behavior of the object. DIAdem saves this tag with the layout. |

| [`IRepClickedPositionInt.X`](irepclickedpositionint-x.md) | Specifies the x-cursor coordinates as page coordinates in DIAdem REPORT when DIAdem calls the event assigned to the OnAxisSystem2D for ClickedWithKeyEvents property. DIAdem calls this event when you click a 2D axis system while pressing a key. For this event DIAdem does not support keys such as <Alt>, <Ctrl>, and <Shift>. Use the methods ConvertPageXPositionToXAxisValue and ConvertPageYPositionToYAxisValue to convert the page coordinates into coordinates of a 2D axis system. |
| [`IRepClickedPositionInt.Y`](irepclickedpositionint-y.md) | Specifies the y-cursor coordinates as page coordinates in DIAdem REPORT when DIAdem calls the event assigned to the OnAxisSystem2D for ClickedWithKeyEvents property. Use the methods ConvertPageXPositionToXAxisValue and ConvertPageYPositionToYAxisValue to convert the page coordinates into coordinates of a 2D axis system. |

| [`IRepD2AxisSettingsInt.AxisScaleMode`](irepd2axissettingsint-axisscalemode.md) | Specifies which method DIAdem uses to scale a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. If you assign the value e2DAxisScalingModeForScaledOutput to the AxisScaleMode property, DIAdem uses the given units per unit length for axis scaling. If, for example, you select 5 units per cm and you represent 60 units, the axis length is 12 cm. Since for automatic scaling DIAdem selects values such as 1, 2, 5, 10, 20, ... for the units per unit length, it is possible that DIAdem uses only part of the axis system to display the curve. If you assign the value e2DAxisScalingModeRangeOfValues to the AxisScaleMode property, DIAdem uses the entire value range of all displayed channels for scaling during automatic scaling. To display the curve, DIAdem uses the entire axis area. You cannot see from the scale settings how many units per unit length DIAdem uses for axis scaling. |

| [`IRepD2AxisXScalingInt.Tick`](irepd2axisxscalingint-tick.md) | Specifies the tick properties of the x-axis in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXScalingInt.Type`](irepd2axisxscalingint-type.md) | Specifies how DIAdem REPORT scales the x-axis of a 2D axis system. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXTickDisplayInt.Size`](irepd2axisxtickdisplayint-size.md) | Specifies the length of the ticks of the x-axis of a 2D axis system as a percentage of the height of the axis system in DIAdem REPORT. DIAdem only includes the property Size if you assign the value FALSE to the UseAutoSize property. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXTickDisplayInt.Type`](irepd2axisxtickdisplayint-type.md) | Specifies on which side of the x-axis DIAdem REPORT plots the axis ticks in a 2D axis system. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXTickDisplayInt.UseAutoSize`](irepd2axisxtickdisplayint-useautosize.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT determines the length of the x-axis ticks in a 2D axis system automatically. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXTickInt.Channel`](irepd2axisxtickint-channel.md) | Specifies the tick channel for the x-axis scaling of a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXTickInt.Distance`](irepd2axisxtickint-distance.md) | Specifies in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT the interval between the ticks you want labeled on the x-axis, in units of the axis range. If the scaling is not logarithmic, the value of the Distance property is the space between the main ticks you want to label. If the scaling is logarithmic, DIAdem interprets the values before the decimal point and the values after the decimal point of the Distance property separately. The integer value before the decimal point specifies the steps between two labels, which are powers of ten. For example, if the axis origin and the tick interval have the value 1, DIAdem labels the ticks at 10 0 , 10 1 , 10 2 and so on. For example, if you assign the value 3 to the tick interval, DIAdem labels the ticks at 10 0 , 10 3 , 10 6 and so on. The reciprocal value after the decimal point, specifies intervals that you want to label in the ranges defined by the value before the decimal point. For example, if you assign the value 1.25 to the Distance property, DIAdem divides the area into quarters. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXTickInt.Origin`](irepd2axisxtickint-origin.md) | Specifies the x-value where DIAdem REPORT plots the first tick when you scale 2D axes manually. |
| [`IRepD2AxisXTickInt.SpacingType`](irepd2axisxtickint-spacingtype.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT takes the positions of the scaling ticks of the x-axis from a data channel or calculates the positions automatically. |
| [`IRepD2AxisYInt.DisableCurveClipping`](irepd2axisyint-disablecurveclipping.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT continues the curve outside the y-axis area of a 2D axis system. |
| [`IRepD2AxisYInt.Height`](irepd2axisyint-height.md) | Specifies the height of the y-subaxis in relation to the first y-axis as a percentage of the length of the original axis in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD2AxisYInt.Index`](irepd2axisyint-index.md) | Specifies the index of a y-axis in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD2AxisYInt.Label`](irepd2axisyint-label.md) | Specifies the label of the y-axis in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD2AxisYInt.Line`](irepd2axisyint-line.md) | Specifies the line properties of the y-axis in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. Assign the value TRUE to the property UseIndividualAxisStyle in order to assign different properties to the axes of a 2D axis system. |
| [`IRepD2AxisYInt.Name`](irepd2axisyint-name.md) | Specifies the name of a y-axis in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |

Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the object. The tag does not affect the behavior of the object. DIAdem saves this tag with the layout. |

If you assign a value to the property TargetUnit , DIAdem converts the channels you want to display into this unit. If DIAdem cannot convert the unit, DIAdem does not display the data. |

| [`IRepD2PaletteInt.BeginValue`](irepd2paletteint-beginvalue.md) | Specifies the lower limit of the y-range in which DIAdem REPORT displays a curve with a color palette. The EndValue property specifies the upper limit of this y-range. |
| [`IRepD2PaletteInt.Channel`](irepd2paletteint-channel.md) | Specifies the channel with the values that DIAdem uses to display the curve in the colors of the palette. DIAdem only includes this color channel if the property ValueType has the value e2DPaletteValueTypeWithChnMinMaxRange , e2DPaletteValueTypeWithChnInputInterval or e2DPaletteValueTypeWithChnInputValueRange . |
| [`IRepD2PaletteInt.EndValue`](irepd2paletteint-endvalue.md) | Specifies the upper limit of the y-range in which DIAdem REPORT displays a curve with a color palette. The BeginValue property specifies the lower limit of this y-range. |
| [`IRepD2PaletteInt.Lines`](irepd2paletteint-lines.md) | Specifies the line properties of a palette in a 2D axis systems or a polar axis systems in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD2PaletteInt.ValueType`](irepd2paletteint-valuetype.md) | Specifies how DIAdem REPORT assigns the colors from the color palette to the curve in a 2D axis system. If the property ValueType has the value e2DPaletteValueTypeAxisScalingRange , e2DPaletteValueTypeDistanceOfAxisTicks , or e2DPaletteValueTypeInputInterval , the colors are the same as the colors of the y-ranges of the curve. For other values, use the Channel property to specify a color channel, which DIAdem uses for displaying the curve in the palette colors. |

| [`IRepD2SegmentInt.Orientation`](irepd2segmentint-orientation.md) | Specifies the alignment of the segments a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |

| [`IRepD2SegmentInt.YChannel`](irepd2segmentint-ychannel.md) | Specifies the data channel with the y-values of the segments when displaying background segments in a 2D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |

If you assign a value to the TargetUnit property, DIAdem converts the channels you want to display into this unit. If DIAdem cannot convert the unit, DIAdem does not display the data. You cannot convert the units if data for a curve entry is available in the form of a matrix. |
| [`IRepD3AxisXInt.TickType`](irepd3axisxint-ticktype.md) | Specifies how DIAdem REPORT plots the scale ticks of the x-axis in a 3D axis system. |

| [`IRepD3BoundaryCurveAdditionalInt.AddFullLoadLowerBoundary`](irepd3boundarycurveadditionalint-addfullloadlowerboundary.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT also displays a full load curve when displaying characteristic diagrams in a 3D axis system. To close the full load curve, DIAdem searches for the smallest and largest x-value of the full load curve. DIAdem connects the points belonging to these two values with a horizontal line at the height of the point with the smaller y-value. DIAdem uses a vertical line to connect the point with the larger y-value with the horizontal line. |

| [`IRepD3CurveInt.Name`](irepd3curveint-name.md) | Specifies the name of a curve in a 3D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD3CurveInt.OnCurveTransformation`](irepd3curveint-oncurvetransformation.md) | Specifies the name of the user command that DIAdem REPORT executes to transform a curve while plotting. The parameter of the user command corresponds to a D3CurveTransformingContext object and provides information about the 3D axis system, the worksheet, and the channels and their data type. Use this property only to manipulate the data of the input channels. REPORT objects such as the worksheet, the axis system, and the curves can only be accessed in read-only mode. Use the curve transformation function to modify the displayed channels while they are being plotted. DIAdem does not modify the original data. The transformed channels have the same display format as the original channels. For example, you cannot create a numeric channel from a time channel using the curve transformation. If you do not specify an x-channel and the y-channel is an xy-channel and you have selected the setting When plotting xy-channels, determine x-channel automatically if not populated in the General DIAdem Settings , you can also transform the x-channel that belongs to the y-channel. The display format remains the same. DIAdem REPORT saves this property with the layout. |
| [`IRepD3CurveInt.RelatedLegendText`](irepd3curveint-relatedlegendtext.md) | Specifies the curve-related text in a 3D axis system legend in DIAdem REPORT. To assign new text to the RelatedLegendText property in Python, use the syntax SetRelatedLegendText( Column , NewText ) . |
| [`IRepD3CurveInt.Shape`](irepd3curveint-shape.md) | Specifies the display mode of a 3D curve in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD3CurveInt.ShapeType`](irepd3curveint-shapetype.md) | Specifies the display mode of a curve in a 3D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. You can use the ChangeShape for 3DCurves method to change the display mode. |
| [`IRepD3CurveInt.TagStored`](irepd3curveint-tagstored.md) | Specifies a tag for an object in DIAdem REPORT. Use this property to add additional information to the object. Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the object. The tag does not affect the behavior of the object. DIAdem saves this tag with the layout. |
| [`IRepD3CurveInt.TagTemporary`](irepd3curveint-tagtemporary.md) | Specifies a temporary tag for an object in DIAdem REPORT. Use this property to add additional information to the object. Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the object. The tag does not affect the behavior of the object. DIAdem does not save this tag with the layout. |
| [`IRepD3CurveInt.VisibleInLegend`](irepd3curveint-visibleinlegend.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays the legend entry of a curve in a 3D axis system. |

| [`IRepD3CurveTransformingContextInt.Curve`](irepd3curvetransformingcontextint-curve.md) | Specifies the curve for the curve transformation in a 3D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD3CurveTransformingContextInt.DataContext`](irepd3curvetransformingcontextint-datacontext.md) | Specifies the number of the input and output channels or the values of the input and output constants for the curve transformation in a 3D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD3CurveTransformingContextInt.DataType`](irepd3curvetransformingcontextint-datatype.md) | Specifies the type of data assignment for the curve transformation in a 3D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD3CurveTransformingContextInt.Sheet`](irepd3curvetransformingcontextint-sheet.md) | Specifies the worksheet for the curve transformation in a 3D axis system in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.DataReductionMode`](irepd3interpolationint-datareductionmode.md) | Specifies in the data reduction of the display points of a 3D axis system in the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram whether DIAdem displays the greatest or the smallest point of a grid cell. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.DataReductionResolution`](irepd3interpolationint-datareductionresolution.md) | Specifies the grid resolution in the data reduction of the display points of a 3D axis system in the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram . The coarser the grid, the faster the display. In many cases the differences between the different resolutions are hardly visible. DIAdem only includes the property DataReductionResolution if you assigned the value e3DDataReductionTypeGrid to the DataReductionType property . |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.DataReductionType`](irepd3interpolationint-datareductiontype.md) | Specifies whether and how DIAdem performs a data reduction of the display points of a 3D axis system in the display type Area or Map in DIAdem-REPORT. The data reduction enables DIAdem to display the triple data much faster. In many cases, the data reduction only marginally changes the display. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.Enable`](irepd3interpolationint-enable.md) | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT executes a surface interpolation of the input data in the display modes Surface and Characteristic diagram in a 3D axis system. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.InterpolationMode`](irepd3interpolationint-interpolationmode.md) | Specifies which method DIAdem uses to interpolate the points of a curve interpolation in a 3D axis system with the display type Surface or Characteristic diagram in DIAdem REPORT. The two methods differ regarding computing time and results. With the standard number of approximately 50 evaluation points the computing time of both interpolation methods is nearly the same. The computing time of the SCADI increases quadratically with the number of evaluation points and is nearly twice as high as the computing time of the SISPL method when approximately 100 evaluation points are used. In contrast, the computing time of the SISPL method is hardly influenced by the number of evaluation points. If there are many points evenly distributed across the surface, both interpolation methods return nearly identical results. However, if there are only a few points or some values are missing, especially near the edges, the interpolation results differ. The SCADI method extends the existing values at the gaps by continuing the neighboring points’ gradient, whereas the SISPL method extends the existing surface down to the x/y plane to the height of the minimum points. The result of the SISPL resembles an elastic surface which is stretched over the x/y plane and is pulled upwards at the evaluation points. The result of the SCADI resembles a rigid surface which runs through the evaluation points. You can only use the e3DInterpolationModeLinear setting if the TripletStructure for 3DCharacteristicDiagram property contains the e3DCharacteristicTripletStructurePartialLoad value. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.ValueRedundancyMode`](irepd3interpolationint-valueredundancymode.md) | Specifies how DIAdem combines triplet points whose x-values and y-values are close to each other, in a surface interpolation. If the data is in a triplet structure, the x-values and y-values are grouped into new x-channels and y-channels respectively, and the z-values are saved as a matrix. During data acquisition several quasi identical (x,y)-points might have been acquired. Therefore you must specify a tolerance when you convert data so that values which deviate due to measurement inaccuracies are saved only once in the matrix. You can select whether DIAdem uses the lowest, the highest, or the average value, whether DIAdem uses the first or the last value in a channel list, or whether DIAdem summates all values within the specified tolerance. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.ValueRedundancyTolerance`](irepd3interpolationint-valueredundancytolerance.md) | Specifies the tolerance as a percentage of the total x-area and y-area within which DIAdem REPORT combines the x- and y-value pairs to one value pair when interpolating a surface. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.XBegin`](irepd3interpolationint-xbegin.md) | Specifies the minimum grid point in x-direction for the curve interpolation of a 3D axis system in the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram in DIAdem REPORT, if you assign the value e3DEvaluationPointsManual to the XMode property. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.XEnd`](irepd3interpolationint-xend.md) | Specifies the maximum grid point in x-direction for the curve interpolation of a 3D axis system in the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram in DIAdem REPORT, if you assign the value e3DEvaluationPointsManual to the XMode property. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.XIntervalCount`](irepd3interpolationint-xintervalcount.md) | Specifies the number of grid points for the curve interpolation of a 3D axis system with the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram in DIAdem REPORT if you assign the value e3DEvaluationPointsManual to the XMode property. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.XMode`](irepd3interpolationint-xmode.md) | Specifies how DIAdem REPORT specifies the origin of the grid points in x-direction for the curve interpolation of a 3D axis system in the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram . |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.YBegin`](irepd3interpolationint-ybegin.md) | Specifies the minimum grid point in y-direction for the curve interpolation of a 3D axis system in the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram in DIAdem REPORT, if you assign the value e3DEvaluationPointsManual to the YMode property. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.YEnd`](irepd3interpolationint-yend.md) | Specifies the maximum grid point in y-direction for the curve interpolation of a 3D axis system in the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram in DIAdem REPORT, if you assign the value e3DEvaluationPointsManual to the YMode property. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.YIntervalCount`](irepd3interpolationint-yintervalcount.md) | Specifies the number of grid points for the curve interpolation in a 3D axis system with the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram in DIAdem REPORT, if you assign the value e3DEvaluationPointsManual to the YMode property. |
| [`IRepD3InterpolationInt.YMode`](irepd3interpolationint-ymode.md) | Specifies how DIAdem REPORT specifies the origin of the grid points in y direction, for the curve interpolation of a 3D axis system with the display modes Surface or Characteristic diagram . |

You must assign the value eMarkerRepetitionEveryNPercent to the property RepetitionMode in order to use the MarkerPercentInterval property. |

| [`IRepExpansionSettingsInt.Mode`](irepexpansionsettingsint-mode.md) | Specifies in which order DIAdem REPORT expands channels in a 2D axis system. If you assign the value eCurveExpansionModeSortByGroups to the Mode property, DIAdem REPORT first plots all original curves and then the expanded curves. If you assign the value eCurveExpansionModeSortByChannels to the Mode variable, DIAdem first plots the first curve and the associated expanded curves and the other curves in the same order. |

If the filling effect relates to the axis, DIAdem REPORT does not use the entire color spectrum of a color shading for shorter curves. In this case, however, it is easier to compare different curves. |

Use the methods ConvertPageXPositionToXAxisValue , and ConvertPageYPositionToYAxisValue to convert the page coordinates of a polar axis system. |

| [`IRepPositionBordersInt.Bottom`](ireppositionbordersint-bottom.md) | Specifies in DIAdem REPORT the distance from the bottom edge of an object to the bottom edge of the worksheet as a percentage of the page area, in cm, or in inch, if you use margins to position the object. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |
| [`IRepPositionBordersInt.Height`](ireppositionbordersint-height.md) | Specifies, in DIAdem REPORT, the height of an object as a percentage of the page area, in cm or in inches, if you use the margins to position the object. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |
| [`IRepPositionBordersInt.Left`](ireppositionbordersint-left.md) | Specifies, in DIAdem REPORT, the distance from the left edge of an object to the left edge of the worksheet as a percentage of the page area, in cm, or in inch, if you use margins to position the object. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |
| [`IRepPositionBordersInt.Right`](ireppositionbordersint-right.md) | Specifies, in DIAdem REPORT, the distance from the right edge of an object to the right edge of the worksheet as a percentage of the page area, in cm, or in inch, if you use margins to position the object. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |
| [`IRepPositionBordersInt.Top`](ireppositionbordersint-top.md) | Specifies, in DIAdem REPORT, the distance from the upper edge of an object to the upper edge of the worksheet as a percentage of the page area, in cm or in inch, if you use margins to position the object. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |
| [`IRepPositionBordersInt.Width`](ireppositionbordersint-width.md) | Specifies, in DIAdem REPORT, the width of an object as a percentage of the page area, in cm or in inches, if you use the margins to position the object. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |
| [`IRepPositionCoordinatesInt.Height`](ireppositioncoordinatesint-height.md) | Specifies, in DIAdem REPORT, the height of an object as a percentage of the page area, in cm or in inch, if you position the object using the coordinate of one corner, the height, and the width. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |
| [`IRepPositionCoordinatesInt.Width`](ireppositioncoordinatesint-width.md) | Specifies in DIAdem REPORT the width of an object as a percentage of the page area, in cm or in inches, if you use the coordinates of a corner, and the height and width to position the object. Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |

Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |

Because you can use either the Bottom , Height , Left , Right , Top , and Width for the ObjectPositionDefinedByBorders property, or the Height , Width , X1 , X2 , Y1 , and Y2 for the ObjectPositionDefinedByCoordinates property to specify the position, these properties impact each other and the value of the property set first can be modified by another property. |

| [`IRepReportEventsInt.OnFinalizeSheetRefresh`](irepreporteventsint-onfinalizesheetrefresh.md) | Specifies which user command DIAdem REPORT executes after it refreshes a worksheet. The user command receives a parameter. The parameter receives the Sheet object of the refreshed worksheet. The property applies to all worksheets in a layout. Use the OnFinalizeSheetRefresh for SheetEvents property to use a separate user command for each worksheet. DIAdem REPORT saves this property with the layout. |

| [`IRepReportInt.TagStored`](irepreportint-tagstored.md) | Specifies any label for a layout in DIAdem REPORT. Use this property to add additional information to the layout. Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the layout. The tag does not affect the behavior of the layout. DIAdem saves this tag with the layout. |
| [`IRepReportInt.TagTemporary`](irepreportint-tagtemporary.md) | Specifies any temporary label for a layout in DIAdem REPORT. Use this property to temporarily add additional information to the layout. Afterwards you can evaluate such information in a program, for example, for special treatment of the layout. The tag does not affect the behavior of the layout. DIAdem does not save this tag with the layout. |

| [`IRepReportOnClickedWithKeyInt.OnAxisSystem2D`](irepreportonclickedwithkeyint-onaxissystem2d.md) | Specifies the user command which DIAdem REPORT triggers when you click a 2D axis system while pressing a key. The user command receives a parameter. The parameter corresponds with a D2AxisSystemClickedWithKeyContext object and provides information about the 2D axis system which you clicked while pressing a key. For this event DIAdem does not support keys such as <Alt>, <Ctrl>, and <Shift>. Use the methods ConvertPageXPositionToXAxisValue and ConvertPageYPositionToYAxisValue to convert the page coordinates into coordinates of a 2D axis system. |
| [`IRepReportOnClickedWithKeyInt.OnAxisSystemPolar`](irepreportonclickedwithkeyint-onaxissystempolar.md) | Specifies the user command which DIAdem REPORT triggers when you click a polar axis system while pressing a key. The user command receives a parameter. The parameter corresponds with a PolarAxisSystemClickedWithKeyContext object and provides information about the polar axis system which you clicked while you pressed a key. For this event DIAdem does not support keys such as <Alt>, <Ctrl>, and <Shift>. Use the methods ConvertPageXYPositionToAngle and ConvertPageXYPositionToLength to convert the page coordinates of a polar axis system. |
| [`IRepReportOnDrawingInt.OnAxisSystem2DCurve`](irepreportondrawingint-onaxissystem2dcurve.md) | Specifies the user command that DIAdem REPORT executes when plotting a curve in a 2D axis system. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a D2CurveDrawingContext object and provides information about the 2D axis system and the worksheet into which DIAdem is plotting the curve. The second parameter corresponds to a 2DCurve object and provides information about the curve DIAdem is plotting. This curve is a temporary copy of the curve defined in the axis system. You can change this temporary curve any way you like. After plotting this curve, you can no longer access the temporary 2DCurve object. DIAdem executes the user command that you assigned to the OnAxisSystem2D for DrawingEvents property, just before DIAdem plots the curves. At this point in time DIAdem has already resolved all channel references, and has already expanded the curves and executed actions such as transferring the curve color to the markers. If you, for example, set the curve color in this user command, the user command must also adapt all the correlated colors. DIAdem REPORT saves this property with the layout. The user command is only executed if you use the Enable for CurveExpansionSettings property to enable the expansion mode. |
| [`IRepReportOnDrawingInt.OnAxisSystem3DCurve`](irepreportondrawingint-onaxissystem3dcurve.md) | Specifies the user command that DIAdem REPORT executes when plotting a curve in a 3D axis system. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a D3CurveDrawingContext object and provides information about the 3D axis system and the worksheet into which DIAdem is plotting the curve. The second parameter corresponds to a 3DCurve object and provides information about the curve DIAdem is plotting. This curve is a temporary copy of the curve defined in the axis system. You can change this temporary curve any way you like. After plotting this curve, you can no longer access the temporary 3DCurve object. DIAdem REPORT saves this property with the layout. The user command is only executed if you use the Enable for CurveExpansionSettings property to enable the expansion mode. |
| [`IRepReportOnDrawingInt.OnPolarSystemCurve`](irepreportondrawingint-onpolarsystemcurve.md) | Specifies the user command that DIAdem REPORT executes when plotting a curve in a polar axis system. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a PolarCurveDrawingContext object and provides information about the polar axis system and the worksheet in which DIAdem is plotting the curve. The second parameter corresponds to a PolarCurve object and provides information about the curve DIAdem is plotting. This curve is a temporary copy of the curve defined in the axis system. You can change this temporary curve any way you like. After plotting this curve, you can no longer access the temporary PolarCurve object. DIAdem REPORT saves this property with the layout. The user command is only executed if you use the Enable for CurveExpansionSettings property to enable the expansion mode. |
| [`IRepReportOnDrawingInt.OnTable2DColumn`](irepreportondrawingint-ontable2dcolumn.md) | Specifies the user command that DIAdem REPORT executes when plotting a curve in a 2D table column. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a 2DTableColumnDrawingContext object and provides information about the 2D table and the worksheet into which DIAdem is plotting the curve. The second parameter corresponds to a 2DTableColumn object and provides information about the table column DIAdem is plotting. This table column is a temporary copy of the table column defined in the table. You can change this temporary table column any way you like. After plotting this table column, you can no longer access the temporary 2DTableColumn object. DIAdem REPORT saves this property with the layout. The user command is only executed if you use the Enable for CurveExpansionSettings property to enable the expansion mode. |

| [`IRepReportOnToolTipInt.OnTable2D`](irepreportontooltipint-ontable2d.md) | Specifies the user command which DIAdem REPORT executes when you press the shift key and move the mouse over a 2D table. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a ToolTip2DTableContext object and provides information about the 2D table in DIAdem REPORT. The second parameter is a text and corresponds with the tooltip for display. |
| [`IRepReportOnToolTipInt.OnTable3D`](irepreportontooltipint-ontable3d.md) | Specifies the user command which DIAdem REPORT executes when you press the shift key and move the mouse over a 3D table. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a ToolTip3DTableContext object and provides information about the 3D table in DIAdem REPORT. The second parameter is a text and corresponds with the tooltip for display: |
| [`IRepReportOnToolTipInt.OnText`](irepreportontooltipint-ontext.md) | Specifies the user command which DIAdem REPORT executes when you press the shift key and move the mouse over a text. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a ToolTipTextContext object and provides information about the comment in DIAdem REPORT. The second parameter is a text and corresponds with the tooltip for display. |
| [`IRepSelectedObjectsListInt.Count`](irepselectedobjectslistint-count.md) | Returns the number of the selected objects in DIAdem REPORT. |
| [`IRepSettingsExportInt.Properties`](irepsettingsexportint-properties.md) | Returns in DIAdem REPORT all custom properties for the export of the layout. If you export the layout as an Office file in XML format, or as a PDF-, JPEG-, PNG- or TIFF-file, DIAdem saves these properties as meta properties in the document. Use Document <Data> to access the meta properties in exported documents. |
| [`IRepSettingsExportPropertiesInt.Count`](irepsettingsexportpropertiesint-count.md) | Returns the number of custom properties for the export of a layout or of a master layout in DIAdem REPORT. If you export the layout as an Office file in XML format, or as a PDF-, JPEG-, PNG- or TIFF-file, DIAdem saves these properties as meta properties in the document. Use Document <Data> to access the meta properties in exported documents. |
| [`IRepSettingsExportPropertyInt.DataType`](irepsettingsexportpropertyint-datatype.md) | Specifies the data type of a custom property for the export of the layout or of the master layout in DIAdem REPORT. If you export the layout as an Office file in XML format, or as a PDF-, JPEG-, PNG- or TIFF-file, DIAdem saves these properties as meta properties in the document. Use Document <Data> to access the meta properties in exported documents. The type for the property names name , title , description , and author must be String , and the type for the property name datetime must be time . If you assign the incorrect type to a property name, an error occurs when you export the documents. |
| [`IRepSettingsExportPropertyInt.ExpressionValue`](irepsettingsexportpropertyint-expressionvalue.md) | Receives the evaluated DIAdem expression of a custom property for the export of the layout or of the master layout in DIAdem REPORT. If the property Value for Property does not contain a DIAdem expression, the properties ExpressionValue and Value are the same. If you export the layout as an Office file in XML format, or as a PDF-, JPEG-, PNG- or TIFF-file, DIAdem saves these properties as meta properties in the document. Use Document <Data> to access the meta properties in exported documents. |
| [`IRepSettingsExportPropertyInt.Name`](irepsettingsexportpropertyint-name.md) | Specifies the name of a custom property for the export of the layout or of the master layout in DIAdem REPORT. If you use the same name in the layout and in the associated master layout and you export the layout as an Office file in XML-Format, or as a PDF-, JPEG-, PNG- or TIFF- file, DIAdem saves the properties of the layout as meta properties in the document instead of the properties of the master layout. Use Document <Data> to access the meta properties in exported documents. |
| [`IRepSettingsExportPropertyInt.Value`](irepsettingsexportpropertyint-value.md) | Specifies the value of a custom property for the export of the layout or of the master layout in DIAdem REPORT. The value can also be a DIAdem expression . If the property Value for Property does not contain a DIAdem expression, the properties ExpressionValue and Value are the same. If you export the layout as an Office file in XML format, or as a PDF-, JPEG-, PNG- or TIFF-file, DIAdem saves these properties as meta properties in the document. Use Document <Data> to access the meta properties in exported documents. |

| [`IRepTable2DColumnFooterSettingsInt.OnDrawingCell`](ireptable2dcolumnfootersettingsint-ondrawingcell.md) | Specifies the user command that DIAdem REPORT executes when drawing the footer of a 2D table column. The event starts the user command that you assigned to the OnDrawingCell property. The user command receives two parameters. The first parameter corresponds to a 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCellContext object and provides information about the table, the column, the footer, and the worksheet in which DIAdem is plotting the footer. The second parameter corresponds to a 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCell object and provides information about the cell DIAdem is plotting. This cell is a temporary copy of the cell defined in the table. You can change this temporary cell any way you like. After plotting this cell, you can no longer access the temporary cell object. DIAdem REPORT saves this property in the layout. |

The first parameter corresponds to a 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCellContext object and provides information about the table, the column, the header, and the worksheet in which DIAdem is plotting the header. The second parameter corresponds to a 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCell object and provides information about the cell DIAdem is plotting. This cell is a temporary copy of the cell defined in the table. You can change this temporary cell any way you like. After plotting this cell, you can no longer access the temporary cell object. Refer to Working with Events in DIAdem for more information on events in DIAdem. DIAdem REPORT saves this property in the layout. |

| [`IRepTable2DDrawingCellContextInt.RelativeRow`](ireptable2ddrawingcellcontextint-relativerow.md) | Specifies the relative row number of the cell that DIAdem is plotting in a 2D table in DIAdem REPORT. The relative row number refers to the row displayed in the table so that the count on the second table page also starts with 1 . If you want to use a row number which corresponds to the data channel, use the property Row for 2DTableDrawingCellContext . |
| [`IRepTable2DDrawingCellContextInt.Row`](ireptable2ddrawingcellcontextint-row.md) | Specifies the absolute row number of the cell that DIAdem is plotting in a 2D table in DIAdem REPORT. The absolute row number refers to the row in the data channel. If you want to use the row number that corresponds to the displayed table, use the property RelativeRow for 2DTableDrawingCellContext . |

| [`IRepTable2DDrawingHeaderFooterCellContextInt.Col`](ireptable2ddrawingheaderfootercellcontextint-col.md) | Determines the column number of the currently drawn cell of a header or footer row of a 2D table in DIAdem-REPORT within the user command. The object of type 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCellContext is passed as the first parameter of the user command. In order for the user command to be called when drawing the header or footer, the name of the function must be set in the OnDrawingCell property of the header or footer object of the table column. |
| [`IRepTable2DDrawingHeaderFooterCellContextInt.Sheet`](ireptable2ddrawingheaderfootercellcontextint-sheet.md) | Determines the worksheet of the currently drawn cell of a header or footer row in a 2D table in DIAdem-REPORT within the user command. The object of type 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCellContext is passed as the first parameter of the user command. In order for the user command to be called when drawing the header or footer, the name of the function must be set in the OnDrawingCell property of the header or footer object of the table column. |
| [`IRepTable2DDrawingHeaderFooterCellContextInt.Table`](ireptable2ddrawingheaderfootercellcontextint-table.md) | Determines the table within the user command whose header or footer is currently drawn in DIAdem-REPORT. The object of type 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCellContext is passed as the first parameter of the user command. In order for the user command to be called when drawing the header or footer, the name of the function must be set in the OnDrawingCell property of the header or footer object of the table column. |
| [`IRepTable2DDrawingHeaderFooterCellContextInt.TitleNumber`](ireptable2ddrawingheaderfootercellcontextint-titlenumber.md) | Determines the number of the currently drawn header or footer cell of a 2D table in DIAdem-REPORT within the user command. Up to three titles can be defined in a table. The object of type 2DTableDrawingHeaderFooterCellContext is passed as the first parameter of the user command. In order for the user command to be called when drawing the header or footer, the name of the function must be set in the OnDrawingCell property of the header or footer object of the table column. |
| [`IRepTable2DDrawingHeaderFooterCellInt.BackgroundColor`](ireptable2ddrawingheaderfootercellint-backgroundcolor.md) | Determines the background color of the currently drawn header or footer cell of a 2D table in DIAdem-REPORT within the user command. The user command whose name is specified in the OnDrawingCell property of the header or footer object is called when the cell is drawn, so that you can change the background color of the cell via the BackgroundColor property depending on a condition. |
| [`IRepTable2DDrawingHeaderFooterCellInt.Font`](ireptable2ddrawingheaderfootercellint-font.md) | Determines the font of the currently drawn header or footer cell of a 2D table in DIAdem-REPORT within the user command. The user command, whose name is specified in the OnDrawingCell property of the header or footer object , is called when the cell is drawn so that you can change the font of the cell as required using the Font property. |
| [`IRepTable2DDrawingHeaderFooterCellInt.Value`](ireptable2ddrawingheaderfootercellint-value.md) | Determines the value of the currently drawn header or footer cell of a 2D table in DIAdem-REPORT within the user command. The user command, whose name is specified in the OnDrawingCell property of the header or footer object , is called when the cell is drawn so that you can change the content of the cell as required using the Value property. |

Use the IndexIncrement property if you do not want to display all x-values of a data channel in a 3D table. DIAdem only includes the property IndexIncrement if you assign the value FALSE to the UseAutoIndex property. |
